### SPANISH

# Principios :
# El comando: Get + masculino mayúscula + femenino mayúscula
# Añade Cap al final para tener mayúscula en el texto
# Añade Opp para invertir masculino/femenino
# "fallback_text" permite utilizar una línea de ubicación en caso de que no se cumpla ninguna condición; en este caso, el comando correspondiente en inglés.

## PALABRA ANTES DE ORDEN (SIN ESPACIO ENTRE AMBAS)
# Get_deldela_RealmFull (del/de la delante GetFullName en un rango de título) *TITLE
# Get_ella_RealmFull (el/la delante GetFullName en un rango de título) *TITLE
# Get_alala_RealmFull (Al/A la delante GetFullName en un rango de título) *TITLE
# Get_ella_PrimaryTitleName (el/la delante PrimaryTitle.GetName) *TITLE
# Get_deldela_PrimaryTitleName (del/de la delante PrimaryTitle.GetName…) *TITLE
# Get_alala_PrimaryTitleName (al/a la delante PrimaryTitle.GetName…) *TITLE

# Get_deldela_Title (del/de la delante GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer) *TITLE
# Get_ella_Title (el/la delante GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer) *TITLE
# Get_ElLa_Title (El/La delante GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer) *TITLE
# Get_alala_Title (al/a la delante GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer) *TITLE
# Get_AlAla_Title (Al/A la delante GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer) *TITLE
# Get_deldela_Society (del/de la delante Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_ella_Society (el/la delante Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_ElLa_Society (El/La delante Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_alala_Society (al/a la delante Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_ella_SocietyRank (el/la delante GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_ElLa_SocietyRank (El/La delante GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_alala_SocietyRank (al/a la delante GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_deldela_SocietyRank (del/de la delante GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_ella_JobTitle (el/la delante GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_ElLa_JobTitle (El/La delante GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_deldela_JobTitle (del/de la delante GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_alala_JobTitle (al/a la delante GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_deldela_SelectedIngredient_1 (del/de la delante GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_deldela_SelectedIngredient_2 (del/de la delante GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_ella_SelectedIngredient_1 (el/la delante GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_ella_SelectedIngredient_2 (el/la delante GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_DelDela_HighGod (del/de la delante Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_AlAla_HighGod (al/a la delante Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_ella_HighGod (el/la delante Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_ElLa_HighGod (El/La delante Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_ella_Scripture (el/la delante Religion.GetScriptureName) *RELIGION
# Get_deldela_Scripture (del/de la delante Religion.GetScriptureName) *RELIGION

## REEMPLAZO DE ÓRDENES CODIFICADAS
# GetReligiousGroupPlFemen (Religion.GetGroupName + PlFemen) *RELIGION GROUP
# GetReligiousGroupFemen (Religion.GetGroupName + Fem) *RELIGION GROUP
# GetReligionPlFemen (Religion.GetName + PlFemen) *RELIGION
# GetReligionPlMas (Religion.GetName + PlMas) *RELIGION
# GetReligionMas (Religion.GetName + Ms) *RELIGION
# GetEvilGodDelDela (Religion.GetRandomEvilGodName + DelDela) *RELIGION
# GetCultureMas (Culture.GetName + Ms) *CULTURE
# GetCulturePlFemen (Culture.GetName + PlFemen) *CULTURE
# GetCulturePlMas (Culture.GetName + PlMas) *CULTURE
# GovernmentMas *GOVERNMENT
# GetGovernmentElLaCap *GOVERNMENT

## REMPLAZO DE ÓRDENES PERSONALIZADAS
# GetCapitalHoldingDelDela (GetCapitalHolding + DelDela)
# GetCapitalHoldingAlAla (GetCapitalHolding + AlAla)
# GetHoldingDelDela (GetHolding + DelDela)
# GetHouseOfWorshipDelDela (GetHouseOfWorship + DelDela)
# GetHouseOfWorshipUnUna (GetHouseOfWorship + UnUna)
# GetReligiousPersonMasFemen (GetReligiousPerson + MasFemen)
# GetTrueReligionScriptureNameDelDela (GetTrueReligionScriptureName + DelDela)
# GetTrueReligionHighGodDelDela (GetTrueReligionHighGod + DelDela)
# GetDWSettlementAlAla (GetDWSettlement + AlAla)
# GetComplimentAdjectiveMasFemen (GetComplimentAdjective + PlFemen)
# GetDWReasonToJoinAlterna (alternativa de GetDWReasonToJoin)

## NUEVAS ÓRDENES PERSONALIZADAS
# GetRealmDelDela (del imperio\del reino\de las tierras condales)
# GetVegetalIncapaz (vegetal\incapaz)
# GetPiojoPulga (gusano\larva)

defined_text = {
	name = GetElElla
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetElElla_male
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetElElla_female
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = Get_deldela_RealmFull
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_del_
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_de_la_
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						is_nomadic = yes # Kaganato, Kanato
						AND = {
							is_feudal = yes
							OR = {
								AND = {
									tier = EMPEROR
									OR = {
										culture_group = altaic # Kaganato
										culture = russian # Zarato
									}
								}
								tier = KING # Reino, Kanato, Sultanato
								AND = {
									tier = DUKE # Ducado, Raj, Jarldómr, Beylerbeylicato
									NOT = {
										culture_group = arabic # Emirato
										culture_group = iranian # Satrapía
										culture = mongol # Gran cacicazgo
										culture = russian # Gran Principado
										culture_group = west_african # Emirato
									}
								}
								AND = {
									tier = COUNT # Condado, Emirato (?), Thikana, Marzbanato, Beylicato 
									NOT = {
										culture = mongol # Jefatura
									}
								}
								AND = {
									tier = BARON
									OR = {
										culture = mongol # Taishi
										culture = turkish # Timar
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_tribal = yes
							OR = {
								AND = {
									tier = EMPEROR
									OR = {
										culture_group = altaic # Kaganato
										culture = russian # Zarato
									}
								}
								AND = {
									tier = KING # Reino, Kanato, Sultanato
									NOT = {
										culture = old_saxon # Gran cacicazgo
									}
								}
								AND = {
									tier = DUKE
									OR = {
										culture_group = dravidian_group # Raj
										culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Raj
										culture = norse # Jarldómr
									}
								}
								AND = {
									tier = COUNT
									OR = {
										culture_group = west_african # Emirato (?)
										culture_group = dravidian_group # Thikana
										culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Thikana
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_theocracy = yes
							OR = {
								AND = {
									tier = KING
									OR = {
										religion_group = muslim # Califato
										religion = orthodox # Patriarcado
									}
								}
								AND = {
									tier = COUNT
									religion_group = muslim # Emirato (?)
								}
								AND = {
									tier = BARON # Templo, Vahram, Khalwat
									NOT = {
										religion_group = christian # Obispado
										religion_group = muslim # Mezquita
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				title = d_fraticelli # Papado fatricelli
				title = d_hurufi # Emirato hurufita
				title = d_ibadi # Califato ibadí
				title = d_iconoclast # Patriarcado iconoclasta
				title = d_jewish # Gran sacerdocio judío
				title = d_kharijite # Califato jariyí
				title = d_miaphysite # Papado miafisita
				title = d_monophysite # Papado monofisita
				title = d_monothelite # Patriarcado monotelita
				title = d_nestorian # Patriarcado de Oriente
				title = d_norse_pagan_reformed # Fylkirato
				title = d_paulician # Patriarcado pauliciano
				title = d_shiite # Califato chií
				title = d_sunni # Califato suní
				title = d_yazidi # Emirato yazidí
				title = e_china_west_governor # Protectorado de las Provincias del Oeste
				title = e_hre # Sacro Imperio romano
				title = e_shiite # Califato chií
				title = e_sunni # Califato suní
				title = e_arabia # Imperio árabe
				title = e_bengal # Imperio bengalí
				title = e_byzantium # Imperio bizantino
				title = e_deccan # Imperio decaní
				title = e_il-khanate # Ilkanato
				title = e_latin_empire # Imperio latino
				title = e_mexikha # Imperio azteca
				title = e_mongol_empire # Imperio mongol
				title = e_persia # Imperio persa
				title = e_roman_empire # Imperio romano
				title = e_seljuk_turks # Imperio selyúcida
				title = e_wendish_empire # Imperio wendo
				title = k_papal_state # Papado
				title = k_orthodox # Patriarcado ecuménico
			}
			NOT = {
				title = d_frisian_navy # Flota de cocas del mar del Norte
				title = d_genoese_navy # Flota de galeras genovesas
				title = d_hanseatic_navy # Flota de cocas del Báltico
				title = d_maghreb_corsairs # Corsarios berberiscos
				title = d_venetian_navy # Flota de galeras del Adriático

## CUSTOM ENGLISH COMMANDS WITH ARTICLE OR GENDER

defined_text = {
	name = GetCapitalHoldingDelDela # Returns a suitable name for the main building of your capital
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_FALLBACK_GetCapitalHoldingDelDela
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Castle_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = castle	}
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Castle_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = castle	}
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = KING }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Castle_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = castle	}
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Temple_1
		trigger = { capital_holding = { holding_type = temple	} }
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Nomad_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = nomad }
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Nomad_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = nomad }
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = KING }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Nomad_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = nomad }
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Tribal_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = tribal	}
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Tribal_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = tribal	}
			higher_tier_than = COUNT
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Tribal_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = tribal	}
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_City_1
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = city }
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_City_2
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = city }
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
			NOT = { higher_tier_than = KING }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_City_3
		trigger = {
			capital_holding = { holding_type = city }
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_ES_GetHoldingDelDela_Fallback_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				capital_holding = {
					OR = {
						holding_type = castle
						holding_type = temple
						holding_type = nomad
						holding_type = tribal
						holding_type = city
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
